classGraph) {\n        return (SortedSet<PluginDesc<Transformation<?>>>) (SortedSet<?>) getPluginDesc(classGraph, PluginType.TRANSFORMATION, source);\n    }\n\n    private ClassLoader[] classLoaderOrder(PluginSource source) {\n        // Classgraph will first scan all the class URLs from the provided classloader chain and use said chain during classloading.\n        // We compute and provide the classloader chain starting from the isolated PluginClassLoader to ensure that it adheres\n        // to the child first delegation model used in connect. In addition, classgraph can fail to find URLs from the\n        // application classloader as it uses an illegal reflections access. Providing the entire chain of classloaders\n        // which included the application classloader forces classpath URLs to be scanned separately.\n        List<ClassLoader> classLoaderOrder = new ArrayList<>();\n        ClassLoader cl = source.loader();\n        while (cl != null) {\n            classLoaderOrder.add(cl);\n            cl = cl.getParent();\n        }\n        return classLoaderOrder.toArray(new ClassLoader[0]);\n    }\n\n    @SuppressWarnings({\"unchecked\"})\n    private <T> SortedSet<PluginDesc<T>> getPluginDesc(\n            ScanResult classGraph,\n            PluginType type,\n            PluginSource source\n    ) {\n        ClassInfoList plugins;\n        Class<T> klass = (Class<T>) type.superClass();\n        try {\n            if (klass.isInterface()) {\n                plugins = classGraph.getClassesImplementing(klass.getName());\n            } else {\n                plugins = classGraph.getSubclasses(klass.getName());\n            }\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            log.debug(\"Reflections scanner could not find any {} in {} for URLs: {}\",\n                    type, source, source.urls(), e);\n            return Collections.emptySortedSet();\n        }\n\n        SortedSet<PluginDesc<T>> result = new TreeSet<>();\n        for (Class<? extends T> pluginKlass : plugins.getStandardClasses().loadClasses(klass, true)) {\n            if (!PluginUtils.isConcrete(pluginKlass)) {\n                log.debug(\"Skipping {} in {} as it is not concrete implementation\", pluginKlass, source);\n                continue;\n            }\n            if (pluginKlass.getClassLoader() != source.loader()) {\n                log.debug(\"{} from other classloader {} is visible from {}, excluding to prevent isolated loading\",\n                        pluginKlass, pluginKlass.getClassLoader(), source);\n                continue;\n            }\n            try (LoaderSwap loaderSwap = withClassLoader(source.loader())) {\n                result.add(pluginDesc(pluginKlass, versionFor(pluginKlass), type, source));\n            } catch (ReflectiveOperationException | LinkageError e) {\n                log.error(\"Failed to discover {} in {}: Unable to instantiate {}{}\",\n                        type.simpleName(), source, pluginKlass.getSimpleName(),\n                        reflectiveErrorDescription(e), e);\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n}\n","numLines":167,"startLine":1,"totalLines":167}}}

This makes this classloader a\n * child-first classloader.\n * <p>\n * This class is thread-safe and parallel capable.\n */\npublic class DelegatingClassLoader extends URLClassLoader {\n    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DelegatingClassLoader.class);\n\n    private final ConcurrentMap<String, SortedMap<PluginDesc<?>, ClassLoader>> pluginLoaders;\n    private final ConcurrentMap<String, String> aliases;\n\n    // Although this classloader does not load classes directly but rather delegates loading to a\n    // PluginClassLoader or its parent through its base class, because of the use of inheritance\n    // in the latter case, this classloader needs to also be declared as parallel capable to use\n    // fine-grain locking when loading classes.\n    static {\n        ClassLoader.registerAsParallelCapable();\n    }\n\n    public DelegatingClassLoader(ClassLoader parent) {\n        super(new URL[0], parent);\n        this.pluginLoaders = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();\n        this.aliases = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();\n    }\n\n    public DelegatingClassLoader() {\n        // Use as parent the classloader that loaded this class. But this choice here provides additional flexibility in managed\n        // environments that control classloading differently (OSGi, Spring and others) and don't\n        // depend on the System classloader to load Connect's classes.\n        this(DelegatingClassLoader.class.getClassLoader());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Retrieve the PluginClassLoader associated with a plugin class\n     *\n     * @param name The fully qualified class name of the plugin\n     * @param range The version range of the plugin\n     * @param connectorLoader The ClassLoader of the connector loading this plugin\n     * @return the PluginClassLoader that should be used to load this, or null if the plugin is not isolated.\n     */\n    PluginClassLoader pluginClassLoader(String name, VersionRange range, Optional<ClassLoader> connectorLoader) {\n        if (!PluginUtils.shouldLoadInIsolation(name)) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        SortedMap<PluginDesc<?>, ClassLoader> inner = pluginLoaders.get(name);\n        if (inner == null) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        ClassLoader pluginLoader = findPluginLoader(inner, name, range, connectorLoader);\n        return pluginLoader instanceof PluginClassLoader\n            ? (PluginClassLoader) pluginLoader\n            : null;\n    }\n\n    ClassLoader connectorLoader(String classOrAlias, VersionRange range) {\n        String fullName = aliases.getOrDefault(classOrAlias, classOrAlias);","numLines":100,"startLine":1,"totalLines":275}}}

If the top path contains only java class files,\n   255→     * return the top path itself. This method follows symbolic links to discover archives and\n   256→     * returns the such archives as absolute paths.\n   257→     *\n   258→     * @param topPath the path to use as root of plugin new LinkedList<>();\n   266→        Set<Path> visited = new HashSet<>();\n   267→\n   268→        if (isArchive(topPath)) {\n   269→            return Collections.singletonList(topPath);\n   270→ dfs.peek().iterator;\n   281→                if (!neighbors.hasNext()) {\n   282→                    dfs.pop().stream.close();\n   283→                    continue;\n   284→                }\n   285→\n   286→                Path adjacent = neighbors.next();\n   287→                if (Files.isSymbolicLink(adjacent)) {\n   288→                    try {\n   289→                        Path symlink = Files.readSymbolicLink(adjacent);\n   290→                        // if symlink is absolute resolve() returns the absolute symlink itself\n   291→                        Path parent = adjacent.getParent();\n   292→                        if (parent == null) {\n   293→                            continue;\n   294→                        }\n   295→                        Path absolute = parent.resolve(symlink).toRealPath();\n   296→                        if (Files.exists(absolute)) {\n   297→                            adjacent = absolute;\n   298→                        } else {\n   299→                            continue;\n   300→                        }\n   301→                    } catch (IOException e) {\n   302→                        // See https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-6288 for a reported\n   303→                        // failure. Such a failure at this stage is not easily reproducible and\n   304→                        // therefore an exception is caught and ignored after issuing a\n   305→                        // warning. This allows class scanning to continue for non-broken plugins.\n   306→                        log.warn(\n   307→                                \"Resolving symbolic link '{}' failed. Ignoring this path.\",\n   308→                                adjacent,\n   309→                                e\n   310→                        );\n   311→                        continue;\n   312→                    }\n   313→                }\n   314→\n   315→                if (!visited.contains(adjacent)) {\n   316→                    visited.add(adjacent);\n   317→                    if (isArchive(adjacent)) {\n   318→                        archives.add(adjacent);\n   319→                    } else if (isClassFile(adjacent)) {\n   320→                        containsClassFiles = true;\n   321→                    } else {\n   322→                        DirectoryStream<Path> listing = Files.newDirectoryStream(\n   323→                                adjacent,\n   324→                                PLUGIN_PATH_FILTER\n   325→                        );\n   326→                        dfs.push(new DirectoryEntry(listing));\n   327→                    }\n   328→                }\n   329→            }\n   330→        } finally {\n   331→            while (!dfs.isEmpty()) {\n   332→                dfs.pop().stream.close();\n   333→            }\n   334→        }\n   335→\n   336→        if (containsClassFiles) {\n   337→            if (archives.isEmpty()) {\n   338→                return Collections.singletonList(topPath);\n   339→            }\n   340→            log.warn(\"Plugin path contains both java archives and class files. Returning only the\"\n   341→                    + \" archives\");\n   342→        }\n   343→        return Arrays.asList(archives.toArray(new Path[0]));\n   344→    }\n   345→\n   346→    public static Set<PluginSource> pluginSources(Set<Path> pluginLocations, ClassLoader classLoader, PluginClassLoaderFactory factory) {\n   347→        Set<PluginSource> pluginSources = new LinkedHashSet<>();\n   348→        for (Path pluginLocation : pluginLocations) {\n   349→            try {\n   350→                pluginSources.add(isolatedPluginSource(pluginLocation, classLoader, factory));\n   351→            } catch (InvalidPathException | MalformedURLException e) {\n   352→                log.error(\"Invalid path in plugin path: {}. 359→    }\n   360→\n   361→    public static PluginSource isolatedPluginSource(Path pluginLocation, ClassLoader parent, PluginClassLoaderFactory factory) throws IOException {\n   362→        List<URL> pluginUrls = new ArrayList<>();\n   363→        List<Path> paths = pluginUrls(pluginLocation);\n   364→        // Infer the type of the source\n   365→        PluginSource.Type type;\n   366→     } else {\n   370→                type = PluginSource.Type.CLASS_HIERARCHY;\n   371→            }\n   372→        } else {\n   373→            type = PluginSource.Type.MULTI_JAR;\n   374→ 384→        return new PluginSource(pluginLocation, type, loader, urls);\n   385→    }\n   386→\n   387→    public static PluginSource classpathPluginSource(ClassLoader classLoader) {\n   388→ PluginSource(null, PluginSource.Type.CLASSPATH, classLoader, parentUrls.toArray(new URL[0]));\n   392→    }\n   393→\n   394→    /**\n   395→     * Return the simple class name of a plugin as {@code a sophisticated Java plugin architecture with interface-based dependency injection. Here are the key components:\\n\\n## Core Plugin Loading System\\n\\nThe plugin loading mechanism is centered in the `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/` package:\\n\\n1. **PluginClassLoader** (PluginClassLoader.java): A custom URLClassLoader that implements child-first class loading for isolating plugin dependencies. It extends URLClassLoader and is thread-safe and parallel capable.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (DelegatingClassLoader.java): Manages multiple PluginClassLoader instances, delegating class loading to appropriate plugin classloaders based on plugin names and versions. It maintains mappings of plugins to their classloaders.\\n\\n3. **Plugins** (Plugins.java): The main entry point for plugin management. It handles:\\n   - Plugin discovery and initialization via `initLoaders()`\\n   - Plugin instantiation through methods like `newConnector()`, `newConverter()`, `newHeaderConverter()`\\n   - Dependency injection by calling `configure()` on instantiated plugins\\n   - Version management for plugins\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery/Scanning\\n\\n1. **PluginScanner** (PluginScanner.java): Abstract base class for plugin discovery implementations\\n   - Entry point: `discoverPlugins(Set<PluginSource>)` method\\n   - Loads JDBC drivers as part of scanning\\n\\n2. **ReflectionScanner** (ReflectionScanner.java): Legacy discovery strategy using ClassGraph library\\n   - Scans classpath for concrete, public classes with no-args constructors\\n   - Checks for subclasses of Connector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate\\n   - Uses `getPluginDesc()` to extract plugin metadata\\n\\n3. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Modern discovery strategy using Java ServiceLoader\\n   - Requires ServiceLoader manifest files (META-INF/services/...)\\n   - More performant than reflection scanning\\n\\n## Plugin Metadata and Type Management\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc** (PluginDesc.java): Encapsulates plugin metadata\\n   - Stores: class, version, type, location, classloader\\n   - Implements Comparable for sorting plugins by version and isolation status\\n\\n2. **PluginType** (PluginType.java): Enum defining plugin categories\\n   - SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER\\n   - TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE\\n   - CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY\\n\\n3. **PluginSource** (PluginSource.java): Represents a source of plugins (JAR, directory, or classpath)\\n\\n4. **PluginScanResult** (PluginScanResult.java): Aggregates plugin discovery results\\n\\n## Plugin Interfaces and Dependency Injection\\n\\nThe system uses interface-based dependency injection where plugins implement standard interfaces and are configured via `configure()` methods:\\n\\n1. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): \\n   - Abstract base class for all connectors\\n   - Receives configuration via `start(Map<String, String> props)`\\n   - Extends Versioned interface\\n\\n2. **SinkConnector** & **SourceConnector**: \\n   - Extend Connector for sink and source workflows\\n\\n3. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java):\\n   - Interface with `configure(Map<String, ?> configs, boolean isKey)` method\\n   - Handles serialization/deserialization of Kafka Connect data\\n   - Discovered via ServiceLoader or reflection\\n\\n4. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable interface\\n   - Provides `configure(Map<String, ?> configs)` via Configurable\\n   - Handles header serialization/deserialization\\n\\n5. **Transformation** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable for configuration injection\\n   - Generic interface for message transformations\\n\\n6. **Predicate** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable for configuration injection\\n   - Used to conditionally apply transformations\\n\\n7. **ConnectRestExtension** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtension.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable and Versioned\\n   - Allows registration of custom JAX-RS resources\\n\\n8. **ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable\\n   - Validates connector client configuration overrides\\n\\n## Dependency Injection Pattern\\n\\nThe system uses a two-step instantiation and injection pattern:\\n\\n1. **Instantiation**: `Utils.newInstance(Class<T>)` creates plugin instances using no-args constructors\\n2. **Injection**: Configuration is provided via:\\n   - Direct method calls: `converter.configure(converterConfig, isKey)` for Converter\\n   - Interface method: Implementations of Configurable call `configure(Map<String, ?> configs)` for HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConnectRestExtension, ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy\\n   - Method parameters: Connectors receive configuration in `start(Map<String, String> props)`\\n\\n## Utility Classes\\n\\n- **PluginUtils** (PluginUtils.java): Provides utility methods for plugin path resolution, concrete class checking, plugin location determination, and alias computation\\n- **PluginClassLoaderFactory** & **ClassLoaderFactory**: Factory classes for creating classloaders\\n- **LoaderSwap**: Thread-context classloader swap utility for safe plugin execution\\n- **Configurable** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java): Base interface for dependency injection, requiring `configure(Map<String, ?> configs)` method\\n- **Versioned** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/components/Versioned.java): Interface for versioned components with `version()` method\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":698,"cache_read_input_tokens":69195,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":698},"output_tokens":7,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"9e3d3859-3607-450f-8637-6674ece955d2","uuid":"f379472b-98c1-4b1b-8c63-a747b9331cc2"}

a sophisticated Java plugin architecture with interface-based dependency injection. Here are the key components:\\n\\n## Core Plugin Loading System\\n\\nThe plugin loading mechanism is centered in the `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/` package:\\n\\n1. **PluginClassLoader** (PluginClassLoader.java): A custom URLClassLoader that implements child-first class loading for isolating plugin dependencies. It extends URLClassLoader and is thread-safe and parallel capable.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (DelegatingClassLoader.java): Manages multiple PluginClassLoader instances, delegating class loading to appropriate plugin classloaders based on plugin names and versions. It maintains mappings of plugins to their classloaders.\\n\\n3. **Plugins** (Plugins.java): The main entry point for plugin management. It handles:\\n   - Plugin discovery and initialization via `initLoaders()`\\n   - Plugin instantiation through methods like `newConnector()`, `newConverter()`, `newHeaderConverter()`\\n   - Dependency injection by calling `configure()` on instantiated plugins\\n   - Version management for plugins\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery/Scanning\\n\\n1. **PluginScanner** (PluginScanner.java): Abstract base class for plugin discovery implementations\\n   - Entry point: `discoverPlugins(Set<PluginSource>)` method\\n   - Loads JDBC drivers as part of scanning\\n\\n2. **ReflectionScanner** (ReflectionScanner.java): Legacy discovery strategy using ClassGraph library\\n   - Scans classpath for concrete, public classes with no-args constructors\\n   - Checks for subclasses of Connector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate\\n   - Uses `getPluginDesc()` to extract plugin metadata\\n\\n3. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Modern discovery strategy using Java ServiceLoader\\n   - Requires ServiceLoader manifest files (META-INF/services/...)\\n   - More performant than reflection scanning\\n\\n## Plugin Metadata and Type Management\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc** (PluginDesc.java): Encapsulates plugin metadata\\n   - Stores: class, version, type, location, classloader\\n   - Implements Comparable for sorting plugins by version and isolation status\\n\\n2. **PluginType** (PluginType.java): Enum defining plugin categories\\n   - SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER\\n   - TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE\\n   - CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY\\n\\n3. **PluginSource** (PluginSource.java): Represents a source of plugins (JAR, directory, or classpath)\\n\\n4. **PluginScanResult** (PluginScanResult.java): Aggregates plugin discovery results\\n\\n## Plugin Interfaces and Dependency Injection\\n\\nThe system uses interface-based dependency injection where plugins implement standard interfaces and are configured via `configure()` methods:\\n\\n1. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): \\n   - Abstract base class for all connectors\\n   - Receives configuration via `start(Map<String, String> props)`\\n   - Extends Versioned interface\\n\\n2. **SinkConnector** & **SourceConnector**: \\n   - Extend Connector for sink and source workflows\\n\\n3. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java):\\n   - Interface with `configure(Map<String, ?> configs, boolean isKey)` method\\n   - Handles serialization/deserialization of Kafka Connect data\\n   - Discovered via ServiceLoader or reflection\\n\\n4. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable interface\\n   - Provides `configure(Map<String, ?> configs)` via Configurable\\n   - Handles header serialization/deserialization\\n\\n5. **Transformation** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable for configuration injection\\n   - Generic interface for message transformations\\n\\n6. **Predicate** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable for configuration injection\\n   - Used to conditionally apply transformations\\n\\n7. **ConnectRestExtension** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtension.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable and Versioned\\n   - Allows registration of custom JAX-RS resources\\n\\n8. **ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java):\\n   - Extends Configurable\\n   - Validates connector client configuration overrides\\n\\n## Dependency Injection Pattern\\n\\nThe system uses a two-step instantiation and injection pattern:\\n\\n1. **Instantiation**: `Utils.newInstance(Class<T>)` creates plugin instances using no-args constructors\\n2. **Injection**: Configuration is provided via:\\n   - Direct method calls: `converter.configure(converterConfig, isKey)` for Converter\\n   - Interface method: Implementations of Configurable call `configure(Map<String, ?> configs)` for HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConnectRestExtension, ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy\\n   - Method parameters: Connectors receive configuration in `start(Map<String, String> props)`\\n\\n## Utility Classes\\n\\n- **PluginUtils** (PluginUtils.java): Provides utility methods for plugin path resolution, concrete class checking, plugin location determination, and alias computation\\n- **PluginClassLoaderFactory** & **ClassLoaderFactory**: Factory classes for creating classloaders\\n- **LoaderSwap**: Thread-context classloader swap utility for safe plugin execution\\n- **Configurable** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java): Base interface for dependency injection, requiring `configure(Map<String, ?> configs)` method\\n- **Versioned** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/components/Versioned.java): Interface for versioned components with `version()` method\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
